500MB chunks\n        \n    def split_large_file(self, media_path: Path) -> List[Path]:\n        \"\"\"Split large files into manageable chunks\"\"\"\n        if media_path.stat().st_size < 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024:  # 2GB\n            return [media_path]\n            \n        chunk_files = []\n        output_pattern = self.base_dir / \"temp\" / f\"chunk_%03d_{media_path.name}\"\n        \n        # Use ffmpeg to split the file\n        cmd = [\n            'ffmpeg', '-i', str(media_path), \n            '-c', 'copy',\n            '-map', '0',\n            '-segment_time', '00:10:00',  # 10-minute chunks\n            '-f', 'segment',\n            '-reset_timestamps', '1',\n            str(output_pattern)\n        ]\n        \n        try:\n            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, capture_output=True)\n            \n            # Fallback to original file\n    \n    def extract_audio_from_large_video(self, media_path: Path) -> Path:\n        \"\"\"Extract audio from large video files to reduce processing load\"\"\"\n        audio_path = self.base_dir / \"temp\" / f\"{media_path.stem}_audio.wav\"\n        \n        # 16kHz sample rate\n            '-ac', '1',  # Mono\n            '-y',  # Overwrite output file\n            str(audio_path)\n        ]\n        \n        try:\n            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, capture_output=True)\n            return audio_path\n        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to extract audio from {media_path}: {e}\")\n            raise\n    \n    def cleanup_temp_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up temporary files\"\"\"\n        temp_dir = self.base_dir / \"temp\"\n        for file in temp_dir.glob(\"*\"):\n            try:\n                file.unlink()\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Could not delete temp file {file}: {e}\")\n```\n\n## 2. **Modified Transcription for Large Files**\n\n```python\ndef transcribe_large_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Transcribe large audio files in chunks\"\"\"\n    file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n    \n    # For files over 500MB, use chunked processing\n    if file_size > 500 * 1024 * 1024:\n        return self._transcribe_in_chunks(audio_path)\n    else:\n        return self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n\ndef _transcribe_in_chunks(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Transcribe audio by processing it in chunks\"\"\"\n    chunk_duration = 600  # 10 minutes in seconds\n    full_transcript = []\n    \n    # Get total duration using ffprobe\n    cmd = [\n        'ffprobe', '-i', str(audio_path),\n        '-show_entries', 'format=duration',\n        '-v', 'quiet', '-of', 'csv=p=0'\n    ]\n    \n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, check=True)\n        total_duration = float(result.stdout.strip())\n    except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, ValueError):\n        total_duration = 3600  # Default to 1 hour if unknown\n    \n    # Process in chunks\n    for start_time in range(0, int(total_duration), chunk_duration):\n        end_time = min(start_time + chunk_duration, total_duration)\n        \n        # Extract chunk\n        chunk_path = self.base_dir / \"temp\" / f\"chunk_{start_time}_{audio_path.name}\"\n        cmd = [\n            'ffmpeg', '-i', str(audio_path),\n            '-ss', str(start_time),  # Start time\n            '-to', str(end_time),    # End time\n            '-c', 'copy',\n            '-y',  # Overwrite\n            str(chunk_path)\n        ]\n        \n        try:\n            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, capture_output=True)\n            \n            # Transcribe chunk\n            chunk_transcript = self.transcribe_audio(chunk_path)\n            full_transcript.append(chunk_transcript)\n            \n            # Clean up chunk\n            chunk_path.unlink()\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to process chunk {start_time}-{end_time}: {e}\")\n            continue\n    \n    return \"\\n\".join(full_transcript)\n```\n\n## 3. **Enhanced Media Processing**\n\n```python\ndef process_large_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n    \"\"\"Process large media files with special handling\"\"\"\n    logger.info(f\"Processing large file: {media_path.name} ({media_path.stat().st_size / (1024**3):.2f} GB)\")\n    \n    try:\n        file_handler = LargeFileHandler(self.base_dir)\n        \n        # Extract audio first (reduces processing load)\n        audio_path = file_handler.extract_audio_from_large_video(media_path)\n        \n        # Transcribe audio\n        if audio_path.stat().st_size > 500 * 1024 * 1024:\n            transcript = self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n        else:\n            transcript = self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n        \n        # Analyze content\n        analysis = self.analyze_content(transcript, f\"Analysis of {media_path.name}\")\n        \n        # Save results\n        self.save_results_formatted(media_path, transcript, analysis)\n        \n        # Clean up\n        audio_path.unlink()\n        file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n        \n        logger.info(f\"✅ Completed large file: {media_path.name}\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"❌ Failed to process large file {media_path.name}: {e}\")\n        # Attempt cleanup even on failure\n        try:\n            file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n        except:\n            pass\n```\n\n## 4. **Memory-Optimized Processing**\n\n```python\ndef optimize_for_memory(self):\n    \"\"\"Configure services for memory-efficient processing\"\"\"\n    # For AssemblyAI - use async processing for large files\n    if os.getenv(\"ASSEMBLYAI_API_KEY\"):\n        aai.settings.base_url = \"https://api.assemblyai.com/v2\"\n    \n    # For OpenAI - specify smaller models for large files\n    def _transcribe_openai_large(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"OpenAI transcription with memory optimization\"\"\"\n        with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n            # For large files, use async processing if available\n            if audio_path.stat().st_size > 100 * 1024 * 1024:\n                # Create uploadable chunked version\n                transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                    model=\"whisper-1\", \n                    file=audio_file,\n                    response_format=\"verbose_json\",\n                    temperature=0.1  # More deterministic for consistency\n                )\n            else:\n                transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                    model=\"whisper-1\", \n                    file=audio_file,\n                    response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n                )\n                \n        return \"\\n\".join(\n            f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start)} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end)}: {seg.text}\"\n            for seg in transcript.segments\n        )\n```\n\n## 5. **Enhanced Main Function**\n\n```python\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main execution function with large file support\"\"\"\n    print(\"=== ULTIMATE Media Analysis Pipeline ===\")\n    print(\"Multi-API Edition with Large File Support\")\n    \n    base_dir_input = input(\"Enter media directory (press Enter for current): \").strip()\n    base_dir = base_dir_input if base_dir_input else None\n    \n    analyzer = UltimateMediaAnalyzer(base_dir)\n    \n    try:\n        # Process all media files with special handling for large files\n        media_files = []\n        large_files = []\n        \n        for ext in ['*.mp3', '*.mp4', '*.wav', '*.m4a', '*.mov', '*.avi']:\n            found_files = list(Path(analyzer.base_dir).glob(ext))\n            media_files.extend(found_files)\n            \n            # Identify large files\n            for file in found_files:\n                if file.stat().st_size > 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024:  # 2GB\n                    large_files.append(file)\n        \n        print(f\"Found {len(media_files)} media files, {len(large_files)} are large (>2GB)\")\n        \n        # Process large files first with special handling\n        for large_file in large_files:\n            analyzer.process_large_media_file(large_file)\n        \n        # Process regular files\n        regular_files = [f for f in media_files if f not in large_files]\n        for media_file in regular_files:\n            analyzer.process_media_file(media_file)\n        \n        print(f\"\\n✅ Analysis complete! Processed {len(media_files)} files.\")\n        print(\"Check 'transcripts' and 'analysis' folders for results.\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"Pipeline failed: {e}\")\n        print(f\"\\n❌ Error: {e}\")\n```\n\n## 6. **Additional Dependencies**\n\nAdd these to your requirements for handling large files:\n```\nffmpeg-python==0.2.0\n# or if you prefer subprocess approach, ensure ffmpeg is installed on system\n```\n\n## 7. **System Requirements**\n\nFor handling 2GB+ files, ensure your system has:\n- Sufficient storage space (at least 2x the largest file size)\n- FFmpeg installed and available in PATH\n- Adequate RAM (16GB+ recommended)\n- Fast storage (SSD recommended for large file operations)\n\n## 8. **Usage Notes**\n\n1. **Install FFmpeg**:\n   - Windows: Download from https://ffmpeg.org/\n   - macOS: `brew install ffmpeg`\n   - Linux: `sudo apt install ffmpeg`\n\n2. **Monitor Resources** when processing large files\n3. **Consider using a powerful machine** or cloud instance for very large files\n\nThis enhanced implementation will handle your 2GB+ MP4 files by:\n1. if unknown\n        \n        # Process in chunks\n        for start_time in range(0, int(total_duration), chunk_duration):\n            end_time = min(start_time + chunk_duration, total_duration)\n Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n            ],\n            max_tokens=1800,\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content\n\n    def _analyze_gemini(self, content: str, context: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Gemini\"\"\"\n        response = self.gemini_client.generate_content(\n            f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content as a media analyst using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"\n        )\n        return response.text\n\n    def _analyze_groq(self, content: str, context: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Groq (Llama 3.1)\"\"\"\n        response = self.groq_client.chat.completions.create(\n            model=\"llama-3.1-8b-instant\",\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are an expert media analyst. Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n            ],\n            max_tokens=1800,\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content\n\n    def process_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Process a single media file\"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Processing: {media_path.name}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check cache first\n            file_hash = self.get_file_hash(media_path)\n            cached_data = self.check_cache(file_hash)\n            \n            if cached_data:\n                logger.info(f\"Using cached results for {media_path.name}\")\n                self.save_results_formatted(media_path, cached_data[\"transcript\"], cached_data[\"analysis\"])\n                return\n            \n            # Transcribe audio\n            transcript = self.transcribe_audio(media_path)\n            \n            # Analyze content\n            analysis = self.analyze_content(transcript, f\"Analysis of {media_path.name}\")\n            \n            # Save results\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            # Save to cache\n            self.save_to_cache(file_hash, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            logger.info(f\"✅ Completed: {media_path.name}\")\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Failed to process {media_path.name}: {e}\")\n\n    def process_large_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Process large media files with special handling\"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Processing large file: {media_path.name} ({media_path.stat().st_size / (1024**3):.2f} GB)\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check cache first\n            file_hash = self.get_file_hash(media_path)\n            cached_data = self.check_cache(file_hash)\n            \n            if cached_data:\n                logger.info(f\"Using cached results for {media_path.name}\")\n                self.save_results_formatted(media_path, cached_data[\"transcript\"], cached_data[\"analysis\"])\n                return\n            \n            # Extract audio first (reduces processing load)\n            audio_path = self.file_handler.extract_audio_from_large_video(media_path)\n            \n            # Transcribe audio\n            if audio_path.stat().st_size > 500 * 1024 * 1024:\n                transcript = self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n            else:\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n            \n            # Analyze content\n            analysis = self.analyze_content(transcript, f\"Analysis of {media_path.name}\")\n            \n            # Save results\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            # Save to cache\n            self.save_to_cache(file_hash, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            # Clean up\n            audio_path.unlink()\n            self.file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n            \n            logger.info(f\"✅ Completed large file: {media_path.name}\")\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Failed to process large file {media_path.name}: {e}\")\n            # Attempt cleanup even on failure\n            try:\n                self.file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n            except:\n                pass\n\n    def save_results_formatted(self, media_path: Path, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save analysis results in the specific format requested\"\"\"\n        base_name = media_path.stem\n        \n        # Save in the exact format: Analysis {content} || Transcript {content}\n        formatted_content = f\"Analysis {{{analysis}}} || Transcript {{{transcript}}}\"\n        \n        # Save to analysis directory\n        analysis_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_formatted.txt\"\n        analysis_file.write_text(formatted_content, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        # Also save separate files for transcript and analysis\n        transcript_file = self.base_dir / \"transcripts\" / f\"{base_name}_transcript.txt\"\n        transcript_file.write_text(transcript, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        analysis_only_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_analysis.txt\"\n        analysis_only_file.write_text(analysis, encoding='utf-8')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def format_timestamp(seconds: float) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format seconds into MM:SS\"\"\"\n        minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n        seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n        return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n    def process_all_media_files(self, max_workers: int = 2):\n        \"\"\"Process all media files with progress tracking\"\"\"\n        media_files = []\n        large_files = []\n        \n        for ext in ['*.mp3', '*.mp4', '*.wav', '*.m4a', '*.mov', '*.avi']:\n            found_files = list(self.base_dir.glob(ext))\n            media_files.extend(found_files)\n            \n            # Identify large files\n            for file in found_files:\n                if file.stat().st_size > 2 * 1024 * 1024 * 1024:  # 2GB\n                    large_files.append(file)\n        \n        print(f\"Found {len(media_files)} media files, {len(large_files)} are large (>2GB)\")\n        \n        # Process large files first with special handling\n        with tqdm(total=len(large_files), desc=\"Processing large files\") as pbar:\n            for large_file in large_files:\n                self.process_large_media_file(large_file)\n                pbar.update(1)\n                pbar.set_postfix(file=large_file.name[:20])\n        \n        # Process regular files\n        regular_files = [f for f in media_files if f not in large_files]\n        with tqdm(total=len(regular_files), desc=\"Processing regular files\") as pbar:\n            for media_file in regular_files:\n                self.process_media_file(media_file)\n                pbar.update(1)\n                pbar.set_postfix(file=media_file.name[:20])\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main execution function with large file support\"\"\"\n    print(\"=== ULTIMATE Media Analysis Pipeline ===\")\n    print(\"Multi-API Edition with Large File Support\")\n    \n    base_dir_input = input(\"Enter media directory (press Enter for current): \").strip()\n    base_dir = base_dir_input if base_dir_input else None\n    \n    analyzer = UltimateMediaAnalyzer(base_dir)\n    \n    try:\n        # Process all media files\n        analyzer.process_all_media_files()\n        \n        print(f\"\\n✅ Analysis complete!\")\n        print(\"Check 'transcripts' and 'analysis' folders for results.\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"Pipeline failed: {e}\")\n        print(f\"\\n❌ Error: {e}\")\n    finally:\n        # Clean up any remaining temp files\n        analyzer.file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Install required packages first:\n    # pip install openai anthropic google-generativeai groq assemblyai deepgram-sdk python-dotenv requests tenacity tqdm\n    main()\n```\n\n## Key Improvements for Large Files:\n\n1. **Large File Handler Class**: Dedicated class for handling files over 2GB\n2. **Chunked Processing**: Splits large files into manageable chunks\n3. **Audio Extraction**: Extracts audio from video files to reduce processing load\n4. **FFmpeg Integration**: Uses FFmpeg for efficient file manipulation\n5. **Memory Optimization**: Processes large files in chunks to avoid memory issues\n6. **Timeout Handling**: Adds timeouts to prevent hanging processes\n7. **Cache System**: Avoids reprocessing the same files\n8. **Progress Tracking**: Shows progress with tqdm progress bars\n9. **Error Resilience**: Better error handling and cleanup\n10. **Retry Logic**: Automatic retries for failed operations\n\n## Requirements:\n\nInstall these additional packages:\n```\npip install tenacity tqdm\n```\n\nAnd ensure FFmpeg is installed on your system:\n- Windows: Download from https://ffmpeg.org/\n- macOS: `brew install ffmpeg`\n- Linux: `sudo apt install ffmpeg`\n\nThis updated code will efficiently handle your 2GB+ MP4 files while maintaining the output format you specified."

versions:\n\n```python\n#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"\nULTIMATE Media Analysis Pipeline - Multi-API Edition\nEnhanced with large file support (2GB+ MP4s)\nCompatible with Pydantic 2.x\n\"\"\"\n\nimport os\nimport logging\nimport time\nimport json\nimport subprocess\nimport hashlib\nfrom pathlib import Path\nfrom typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List\nfrom dotenv import load_dotenv\n\n# Load environment variables first\nload_dotenv()\n\n# Now import other packages\ntry:\n    from openai import OpenAI\n    import anthropic\n    import google.generativeai as genai\n    import groq\n    import assemblyai as aai\n    import deepgram\n    from tqdm import tqdm\n    import tenacity\nexcept ImportError as e:\n    print(f\"Import error: {e}\")\n    print(\"Please install required packages with: pip install openai anthropic google-generativeai groq assemblyai deepgram-sdk python-dotenv requests tenacity tqdm\")\n    exit(1)\n\n# Configure logging\nlogging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO, format='%(asctime)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s')\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\nclass LargeFileHandler:\n    def __init__(self, base_dir: Path):\n        self.base_dir = base_dir\n        \n    def extract_audio_from_large_video(self, media_path: Path) -> Path:\n        \"\"\"Extract audio from large video files to reduce processing load\"\"\"\n        temp_dir = self.base_dir / \"temp\"\n        temp_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        audio_path = temp_dir / f\"{media_path.stem}_audio.wav\"\n        \n        # Use ffmpeg to extract audio\n        cmd = [\n            'ffmpeg', '-i', str(media_path),\n            '-vn',  # No video\n            '-acodec', 'pcm_s16le',  # PCM audio\n            '-ar', '16000',  # 16kHz sample rate\n            '-ac', '1',  # Mono\n            '-y',  # Overwrite output file\n            str(audio_path)\n        ]\n        \n        try:\n            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, capture_output=True, timeout=1800)  # 30 min timeout\n            return audio_path\n        except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired) as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to extract audio from {media_path}: {e}\")\n            raise\n    \n    def cleanup_temp_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up temporary files\"\"\"\n        temp_dir = self.base_dir / \"temp\"\n        if temp_dir.exists():\n            for file in temp_dir.glob(\"*\"):\n                try:\n                    file.unlink()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    logger.warning(f\"Could not delete temp file {file}: {e}\")\n\nclass UltimateMediaAnalyzer:\n    def __init__(self, base_dir: str = None):\n        self.base_dir = Path(base_dir) if base_dir else Path.cwd()\n        self.setup_directories()\n        self.setup_clients()\n        self.file_handler = LargeFileHandler(self.base_dir)\n        \n    def setup_directories(self):\n        \"\"\"Create all necessary directories\"\"\"\n        directories = [\n            \"transcripts\", \"analysis\", \"temp\", \n            \"summaries\", \"embeddings\", \"exports\", \"cache\"\n        ]\n        for dir_name in directories:\n            (self.base_dir / dir_name).mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Analyzer initialized with base directory: {self.base_dir}\")\n\n    def setup_clients(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize all API clients\"\"\"\n        # Check for API keys first\n        required_keys = {\n            \"OPENAI_API_KEY\": \"OpenAI\",\n            \"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\": \"Anthropic\", \n            \"GEMINI_API_KEY\": \"Google Gemini\",\n            \"GROQ_API_KEY\": \"Groq\",\n            \"ASSEMBLYAI_API_KEY\": \"AssemblyAI\",\n            \"DEEPGRAM_API_KEY\": \"Deepgram\"\n        }\n        \n        missing_keys = []\n        for key, service in required_keys.items():\n            if not os.getenv(key):\n                missing_keys.append(service)\n                logger.warning(f\"API key for {service} not found. Some functionality will be limited.\")\n        \n        if missing_keys:\n            print(f\"Warning: Missing API keys for: {', '.join(missing_keys)}\")\n        \n        # Initialize clients only if API keys are available\n        try:\n            if os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"):\n                self.openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"))\n            else:\n                self.openai_client = None\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"):\n                self.anthropic_client = anthropic.Anthropic(api_key=os.getenv(\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"))\n            else:\n                self.anthropic_client = None\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"GEMINI_API_KEY\"):\n                genai.configure(api_key=os.getenv(\"GEMINI_API_KEY\"))\n                self.gemini_client = genai.GenerativeModel('gemini-pro')\n            else:\n                self.gemini_client = None\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"GROQ_API_KEY\"):\n                self.groq_client = groq.Groq(api_key=os.getenv(\"GROQ_API_KEY\"))\n            else:\n                self.groq_client = None\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"ASSEMBLYAI_API_KEY\"):\n                aai.settings.api_key = os.getenv(\"ASSEMBLYAI_API_KEY\")\n                self.assembly_client = aai.Transcriber()\n            else:\n                self.assembly_client = None\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"DEEPGRAM_API_KEY\"):\n                self.deepgram_client = deepgram.Deepgram(os.getenv(\"DEEPGRAM_API_KEY\"))\n            else:\n                self.deepgram_client = None\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to initialize API clients: {e}\")\n            # Set all clients to None to avoid further errors\n            self.openai_client = None\n            self.anthropic_client = None\n            self.gemini_client = None\n            self.groq_client = None\n            self.assembly_client = None\n            self.deepgram_client = None\n        \n        logger.info(\"API clients initialized\")\n\n    def get_file_hash(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate MD5 hash of file contents\"\"\"\n        with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n            return hashlib.md5(f.read()).hexdigest()\n\n    def check_cache(self, file_hash: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Check if file has been processed before\"\"\"\n        cache_file = self.base_dir / \"cache\" / f\"{file_hash}.json\"\n        if cache_file.exists():\n            try:\n                with open(cache_file, \"r\") as f:\n                    cache_data = json.load(f)\n                # Check if cache is still valid (less than 7 days old)\n                cache_date = time.strptime(cache_data[\"timestamp\"], \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")\n                cache_time = time.mktime(cache_date)\n                if time.time() - cache_time < 7 * 24 * 3600:  # 7 days\n                    return cache_data\n            except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError, KeyError) as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Invalid cache file {cache_file}: {e}\")\n        return None\n\n    def save_to_cache(self, file_hash: str, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save results to cache\"\"\"\n        cache_file = self.base_dir / \"cache\" / f\"{file_hash}.json\"\n        cache_data = {\n            \"timestamp\": time.strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\"),\n            \"transcript\": transcript,\n            \"analysis\": analysis\n        }\n        try:\n            with open(cache_file, \"w\") as f:\n                json.dump(cache_data, f)\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Failed to save cache file {cache_file}: {e}\")\n\n    @tenacity.retry(\n        stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n        wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n    )\n    def transcribe_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe audio using best available service\"\"\"\n        methods = [\n            self._transcribe_openai,\n            self._transcribe_assemblyai,\n            self._transcribe_deepgram,\n            self._transcribe_fallback\n        ]\n        \n        for method in methods:\n            try:\n                result = method(audio_path)\n                if result:\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Transcription method failed: {e}\")\n                continue\n        \n        # If all methods fail, return a basic fallback\n        return self._transcribe_fallback(audio_path)\n\n    def _transcribe_openai(self, audio_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe using OpenAI Whisper\"\"\"\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n                transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                    model=\"whisper-1\", \n                    file=audio_file,\n                    response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n                )\n                return \"\\n\".join(\n                    f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start)} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end)}: {seg.text}\"\n                    for seg in transcript.segments\n                )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"OpenAI transcription failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _transcribe_assemblyai(self, audio_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe using AssemblyAI\"\"\"\n        if not self.assembly_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            transcript = self.assembly_client.transcribe(str(audio_path))\n            if transcript.status == aai.TranscriptStatus.error:\n                return None\n                \n            return \"\\n\".join(\n                f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start)} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end)}: {seg.text}\"\n                for seg in transcript.words\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"AssemblyAI transcription failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _transcribe_deepgram(self, audio_path: Path) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe using Deepgram\"\"\"\n        if not self.deepgram_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio:\n                source = {\"buffer\": audio, \"mimetype\": \"audio/mp3\"}\n                response = self.deepgram_client.transcription.sync_prerecorded(source, {\"punctuate\": True})\n                \n            return response[\"results\"][\"channels\"][0][\"alternatives\"][0][\"transcript\"]\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Deepgram transcription failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _transcribe_fallback(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Fallback transcription\"\"\"\n        logger.warning(\"Using fallback transcription - quality may be lower\")\n        # Return a simple timestamped format\n        return \"00:00 -- 01:00: Audio content transcription unavailable. Please check API keys and connectivity.\"\n\n    def transcribe_large_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe large audio files\"\"\"\n        file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n        \n        # For very large files, use a simple approach\n        if file_size > 500 * 1024 * 1024:\n            logger.info(f\"Processing large audio file: {audio_path.name} ({file_size / (1024**3):.2f} GB)\")\n            # Just use the regular transcription method but with a warning\n            result = self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n            if \"unavailable\" in result:\n                return \"00:00 -- 05:00: Large audio file processing requires API services. Please check your API keys.\"\n            return result\n        else:\n            return self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n\n    @tenacity.retry(\n        stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n        wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n    )\n    def analyze_content(self, content: str, context: str = \"\") -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze content using best available LLM\"\"\"\n        methods = [\n            self._analyze_claude,\n            self._analyze_gpt4,\n            self._analyze_gemini,\n            self._analyze_groq\n        ]\n        \n        for method in methods:\n            try:\n                result = method(content, context)\n                if result and self.validate_analysis_format(result):\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Analysis method failed: {e}\")\n                continue\n        \n        # Fallback to template if all methods fail\n        return self.generate_analysis_template(content)\n\n    def validate_analysis_format(self, analysis: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Validate the analysis output format\"\"\"\n        required_sections = [\n            \"Central Themes and Messages\",\n            \"Emotional Tone\",\n            \"Narrative Arc\",\n            \"Creator's Intent\",\n            \"Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\",\n            \"Storytelling Techniques\", \n            \"Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\",\n            \"Audience Engagement and Impact\",\n            \"Overall Effectiveness\"\n        ]\n        \n        return all(section in analysis for section in required_sections)\n\n    def generate_analysis_template(self, content: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate analysis using template format\"\"\"\n        template = \"\"\"\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\nAnalysis of central themes and messages would appear here.\n\n### 2. Emotional Tone\nAnalysis of emotional tone would appear here.\n\n### 3. Narrative Arc\nAnalysis of narrative arc would appear here.\n\n### 4. Creator's Intent\nAnalysis of creator's intent would appear here.\n\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\nAnalysis of metaphors, symbols, and imagery would appear here.\n\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\nAnalysis of storytelling techniques would appear here.\n\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\nAnalysis of visuals and audio interplay would appear here.\n\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\nAnalysis of audience engagement and impact would appear here.\n\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\nOverall effectiveness assessment would appear here.\n\"\"\"\n        return template\n\n    def _analyze_claude(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Claude 3.5\"\"\"\n        if not self.anthropic_client:\n            return None\n            \n        prompt = f\"\"\"\n        As an expert media analyst, provide comprehensive analysis in this exact format:\n\n        ### 1. Central Themes and Messages\n        [Analyze the central themes and messages]\n\n        ### 2. Emotional Tone\n        [Analyze the emotional tone]\n\n        ### 3. Narrative Arc\n        [Analyze the narrative arc]\n\n        ### 4. Creator's Intent\n        [Analyze the creator's intent]\n\n        ### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\n        [Analyze metaphors, symbols, and imagery]\n\n        ### 6. Storytelling Techniques\n        [Analyze storytelling techniques]\n\n        ### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\n        [Analyze the interplay between visuals and audio]\n\n        ### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\n        [Analyze audience engagement and impact]\n\n        ### 9. Overall Effectiveness\n        [Provide overall assessment of effectiveness]\n\n        Context: {context}\n        Content: {content}\n        \"\"\"\n        \n        try:\n            message = self.anthropic_client.messages.create(\n                model=\"claude-3-5-sonnet-20240620\",\n                max_tokens=2000,\n                messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}]\n            )\n            return message.content[0].text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Claude analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _analyze_gpt4(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using GPT-4\"\"\"\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            response = self.openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4o\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are an expert media analyst. Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1800,\n            )\n            return response.choices[0].message.content\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"GPT-4 analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _analyze_gemini(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Gemini\"\"\"\n        if not self.gemini_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            response = self.gemini_client.generate_content(\n                f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content as a media analyst using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"\n            )\n            return response.text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Gemini analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _analyze_groq(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Groq (Llama 3.1)\"\"\"\n        if not self.groq_client:\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            response = self.groq_client.chat.completions.create(\n                model=\"llama-3.1-8b-instant\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are an expert media analyst. Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1800,\n            )\n            return response.choices[0].message.content\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Groq analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def process_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Process a single media file\"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Processing: {media_path.name}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check cache first\n            file_hash = self.get_file_hash(media_path)\n            cached_data = self.check_cache(file_hash)\n            \n            if cached_data:\n                logger.info(f\"Using cached results for {media_path.name}\")\n                self.save_results_formatted(media_path, cached_data[\"transcript\"], cached_data[\"analysis\"])\n                return\n            \n            # For large video files, extract audio first\n            if media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp4', '.mov', '.avi'] and media_path.stat().st_size > 100 * 1024 * 1024:  # 100MB\n                audio_path = self.file_handler.extract_audio_from_large_video(media_path)\n                transcript = self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n                # Clean up audio file\n                audio_path.unlink()\n            else:\n                # For smaller files or audio files, process directly\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(media_path)\n            \n            # Save to cache\n            self.save_to_cache(file_hash, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            logger.info(f\"✅ Completed: {media_path.name}\")\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Failed to process {media_path.name}: {e}\")\n            # Save error result\n            error_transcript = \"00:00 -- 01:00: Error processing file. Please check logs for details.\"\n            error_analysis = self.generate_analysis_template(\"\")\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, error_transcript, error_analysis)\n\n    def save_results_formatted(self, media_path: Path, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save analysis results in the specific format requested\"\"\"\n        base_name = media_path.stem\n        \n        # Save in the exact format: Analysis {content} || Transcript {content}\n        formatted_content = f\"Analysis {{{analysis}}} || Transcript {{{transcript}}}\"\n        \n        # Save to analysis directory\n        analysis_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_formatted.txt\"\n        analysis_file.write_text(formatted_content, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        # Also save separate files for transcript and analysis\n        transcript_file = self.base_dir / \"transcripts\" / f\"{base_name}_transcript.txt\"\n        transcript_file.write_text(transcript, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        analysis_only_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_analysis.txt\"\n        analysis_only_file.write_text(analysis, encoding='utf-8')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def format_timestamp(seconds: float) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format seconds into MM:SS\"\"\"\n        minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n        seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n        return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n    def process_all_media_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Process all media files with progress tracking\"\"\"\n        media_files = []\n        \n        for ext in ['*.mp3', '*.mp4', '*.wav', '*.m4a', '*.mov', '*.avi']:\n            media_files.extend(self.base_dir.glob(ext))\n        \n        print(f\"Found {len(media_files)} media files\")\n        \n        # Process files with progress bar\n        with tqdm(total=len(media_files), desc=\"Processing files\") as pbar:\n            for media_file in media_files:\n                self.process_media_file(media_file)\n                pbar.update(1)\n                pbar.set_postfix(file=media_file.name[:20])\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main execution function with large file support\"\"\"\n    print(\"=== ULTIMATE Media Analysis Pipeline ===\")\n    print(\"Multi-API Edition with Large File Support\")\n    \n    base_dir_input = input(\"Enter media directory (press Enter for current): \").strip()\n    base_dir = base_dir_input if base_dir_input else None\n    \n    analyzer = UltimateMediaAnalyzer(base_dir)\n    \n    try:\n        # Transcription requires OpenAI API key.\"\n\n    @tenacity.retry(\n        stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n        wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n    )\n    def analyze_content(self, content: str, context: str = \"\") -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze content using best available LLM (Claude preferred, then GPT-4o)\"\"\"\n        # Try Claude first\n        if self.anthropic_client:\n            try:\n                result = self._analyze_claude(content, context)\n                if result and self.validate_analysis_format(result):\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Claude analysis failed: {e}\")\n        \n        # Fall back to GPT-4o if Claude fails or is unavailable\n        if self.openai_client:\n            try:\n                result = self._analyze_gpt4(content, context)\n                if result and self.validate_analysis_format(result):\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"GPT-4 analysis failed: {e}\")\n        \n        # Fallback to template if all methods fail\n        return self.generate_analysis_template(content)\n\n    def validate_analysis_format(self, analysis: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Validate the analysis output format\"\"\"\n        required_sections = [\n            \"Central Themes and Messages\",\n            \"Emotional Tone\",\n            \"Narrative Arc\",\n            \"Creator's Intent\",\n            \"Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\",\n            \"Storytelling Techniques\", \n            \"Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\",\n            \"Audience Engagement and Impact\",\n            \"Overall Effectiveness\"\n        ]\n        \n        return all(section in analysis for section in required_sections)\n\n    def generate_analysis_template(self, content: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate analysis using template format\"\"\"\n        template = \"\"\"\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\nAnalysis of central themes and messages would appear here.\n\n### 2. Emotional Tone\nAnalysis of emotional tone would appear here.\n\n### 3. Narrative Arc\nAnalysis of narrative arc would appear here.\n\n### 4. Creator's Intent\nAnalysis of creator's intent would appear here.\n\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\nAnalysis of metaphors, symbols, and imagery would appear here.\n\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\nAnalysis of storytelling techniques would appear here.\n\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\nAnalysis of visuals and audio interplay would appear here.\n\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\nAnalysis of audience engagement and impact would appear here.\n\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\nOverall effectiveness assessment would appear here.\n\"\"\"\n        return template\n\n    def _analyze_claude(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Claude 3.5\"\"\"\n        prompt = f\"\"\"\n        As an expert media analyst, provide comprehensive analysis in this exact format:\n\n        ### 1. Central Themes and Messages\n        [Analyze the central themes and messages]\n\n        ### 2. Emotional Tone\n        [Analyze the emotional tone]\n\n        ### 3. Narrative Arc\n        [Analyze the narrative arc]\n\n        ### 4. Creator's Intent\n        [Analyze the creator's intent]\n\n        ### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\n        [Analyze metaphors, symbols, and imagery]\n\n        ### 6. Storytelling Techniques\n        [Analyze storytelling techniques]\n\n        ### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\n        [Analyze the interplay between visuals and audio]\n\n        ### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\n        [Analyze audience engagement and impact]\n\n        ### 9. Overall Effectiveness\n        [Provide overall assessment of effectiveness]\n\n        Context: {context}\n        Content: {content}\n        \"\"\"\n        \n        try:\n            message = self.anthropic_client.messages.create(\n                model=\"claude-3-5-sonnet-20240620\",\n                max_tokens=2000,\n                messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}]\n            )\n            return message.content[0].text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Claude analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _analyze_gpt4(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using GPT-4\"\"\"\n        response = self.openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n            model=\"gpt-4o\",\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are an expert media analyst. Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n            ],\n            max_tokens=1800,\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content\n\n    def process_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Process a single media file\"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Processing: {media_path.name}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check cache first\n            file_hash = self.get_file_hash(media_path)\n            cached_data = self.check_cache(file_hash)\n            \n            if cached_data:\n                logger.info(f\"Using cached results for {media_path.name}\")\n                self.save_results_formatted(media_path, cached_data[\"transcript\"], cached_data[\"analysis\"])\n                return\n            \n            # For video files, extract audio first\n            transcript = \"\"\n            if media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp4', '.mov', '.avi']:\n                audio_path = self.file_handler.extract_audio_from_video(media_path)\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n                # Clean up audio file\n                audio_path.unlink()\n            elif media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a']:\n                # For audio files, process directly\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(media_path)\n            else:\n                logger.warning(f\"Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\")\n                transcript = f\"00:00 -- 01:00: Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\"\n            \n            # Save error result\n            error_transcript = \"00:00 -- 01:00: Error processing file. Please check logs for details.\"\n            error_analysis = self.generate_analysis_template(\"\")\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, error_transcript, error_analysis)\n\n    def save_results_formatted(self, media_path: Path, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save analysis results in the specific format requested\"\"\"\n        base_name = media_path.stem\n        \n        # Save in the exact format: Analysis {content} || Transcript {content}\n        formatted_content = f\"Analysis {{{analysis}}} || Transcript {{{transcript}}}\"\n        \n        # Save to analysis directory\n        analysis_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_formatted.txt\"\n        analysis_file.write_text(formatted_content, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        # Here's how it works:\n\n## Current Behavior:\n\n1. **Singular Processing**: Each large file is processed as a single unit\n2. **Audio Extraction**: For video files >100MB, audio is extracted first using FFmpeg\n3. **Direct Transcription**: The extracted audio is sent to OpenAI Whisper for transcription\n4. **No Chunking**: The current code doesn't split large audio files into chunks\n\n## The Issue:\n\nOpenAI Whisper has these limits:\n- **25MB file size limit** for the API\n- **No official chunking support** in the standard API\n\n## Solutions:\n\nHere are 3 approaches to handle 1GB+ files:\n\n### Option 1: Manual Chunking (Recommended)\n\nAdd this method to handle large audio files:\n\n```python\ndef transcribe_large_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Transcribe large audio files by splitting into chunks\"\"\"\n    file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n    \n    # For files under 25MB, use standard transcription\n    if file_size <= 25 * 1024 * 1024:\n        return self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)\n    \n    # For larger files, split into chunks\n    logger.info(f\"Splitting large audio file: {audio_path.name} ({file_size/(1024*1024):.1f}MB)\")\n    \n    # Get audio duration using ffprobe\n    duration = self.get_audio_duration(audio_path)\n    chunk_duration = 600  # 10 minutes per chunk (safe for Whisper)\n    \n    transcripts = []\n    \n    for start_time in range(0, int(duration), chunk_duration):\n        end_time = min(start_time + chunk_duration, duration)\n        \n        # Extract chunk\n        chunk_path = self.base_dir / \"temp\" / f\"chunk_{start_time}_{audio_path.name}\"\n        self.extract_audio_chunk(audio_path, chunk_path, start_time, end_time)\n        \n        # Transcribe chunk\n        try:\n            chunk_transcript = self.transcribe_audio(chunk_path)\n            transcripts.append(chunk_transcript)\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to transcribe chunk {start_time}-{end_time}: {e}\")\n            transcripts.append(f\"[Chunk {start_time}-{end_time}s: Transcription failed]\")\n        \n        # Clean up chunk\n        chunk_path.unlink()\n    \n    return \"\\n\".join(transcripts)\n\ndef get_audio_duration(self, audio_path: Path) -> float:\n    \"\"\"Get audio duration using ffprobe\"\"\"\n    cmd = [\n        'ffprobe', '-i', str(audio_path),\n        '-show_entries', 'format=duration',\n        '-v', 'quiet', '-of', 'csv=p=0'\n    ]\n    \n    try:\n        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, check=True, timeout=30)\n        return float(result.stdout.strip())\n    except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, ValueError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired):\n        # Fall back to manual chunking\n    \n    try:\n        # Use AssemblyAI's async transcription for large files\n        transcriber = aai.Transcriber()\n        transcript = transcriber.transcribe(str(audio_path))\n        \n        if transcript.status == aai.TranscriptStatus.error:\n            raise Exception(transcript.error)\n            \n        return \"\\n\".join(\n            f\"{self.format_timestamp(word.start / 1000)} -- {self.format_timestamp(word.end / 1000)}: {word.text}\"\n            for word in transcript.words\n        )\n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"AssemblyAI transcription failed: {e}\")\n        # Fall back to manual chunking\n        return self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n```\n\n### Option 3: Hybrid Approach\n\nModify the `transcribe_audio` method to handle large files:\n\n```python\n@tenacity.retry(\n    stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n    wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n)\ndef transcribe_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Transcribe audio with large file support\"\"\"\n    file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n    \n    # For small files, use OpenAI directly\n    if file_size <= 25 * 1024 * 1024:  # 25MB\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            return self._transcribe_fallback(audio_path)\n            \n        try:\n            with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n                transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                    model=\"whisper-1\", \n                    file=audio_file,\n                    response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n                )\n                return \"\\n\".join(\n                    f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start)} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end)}: {seg.text}\"\n                    for seg in transcript.segments\n                )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"OpenAI transcription failed: {e}\")\n            # Fall through to chunking method\n    \n    # For large files, use chunking\n    return self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n```\n\n## Updated Process Method:\n\n```python\ndef process_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n    \"\"\"Process a single media file with large file support\"\"\"\n    logger.info(f\"Processing: {media_path.name}\")\n    \n    try:\n        # This now handles large files\n            # Clean up audio file\n            audio_path.unlink()\n        elif media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a']:\n            # For audio files, process directly (with large file support)\n            transcript = self.transcribe_audio(media_path)\n        else:\n            logger.warning(f\"Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\")\n            transcript = f\"00:00 -- 01:00: Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\"\n        \n        # Use ffmpeg to extract audio\n        cmd = [\n            'ffmpeg', '-i', str(media_path),\n            '-vn',  # No video\n            '-acodec', 'pcm_s16le',  # PCM audio\n            '-ar', '16000',  #
