Mono\n            '-y',                    # Overwrite output\n            str(output_path)\n        ]\n        \n        try:\n            subprocess.run(cmd, check=True, capture_output=True, timeout=300)\n        except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, subprocess.TimeoutExpired) as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to extract audio chunk {start_time}-{end_time}: {e}\")\n            raise\n    \n    def cleanup_temp_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Clean up temporary files\"\"\"\n        temp_dir = self.base_dir / \"temp\"\n        if temp_dir.exists():\n            for file in temp_dir.glob(\"*\"):\n                try:\n                    file.unlink()\n                except Exception as e:\n                    logger.warning(f\"Could not delete temp file {file}: {e}\")\n\nclass UltimateMediaAnalyzer:\n    def __init__(self, base_dir: str = None):\n        self.base_dir = Path(base_dir) if base_dir else Path.cwd()\n        self.setup_directories()\n        self.setup_clients()\n        self.file_handler = LargeFileHandler(self.base_dir)\n        \n    def setup_directories(self):\n        \"\"\"Create all necessary directories\"\"\"\n        directories = [\n            \"transcripts\", \"analysis\", \"temp\", \n            \"summaries\", \"embeddings\", \"exports\", \"cache\"\n        ]\n        for dir_name in directories:\n            (self.base_dir / dir_name).mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Analyzer initialized with base directory: {self.base_dir}\")\n\n    def setup_clients(self):\n        \"\"\"Initialize only GPT-4o and Claude clients\"\"\"\n        # Check for API keys first\n        required_keys = {\n            \"OPENAI_API_KEY\": \"OpenAI\",\n            \"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\": \"Anthropic\"\n        }\n        \n        missing_keys = []\n        for key, service in required_keys.items():\n            if not os.getenv(key):\n                missing_keys.append(service)\n                logger.warning(f\"API key for {service} not found. Functionality will be limited.\")\n        \n        if missing_keys:\n            print(f\"Warning: Missing API keys for: {', '.join(missing_keys)}\")\n        \n        # Initialize clients only if API keys are available\n        try:\n            if os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"):\n                self.openai_client = OpenAI(api_key=os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\"))\n                logger.info(\"OpenAI client initialized\")\n            else:\n                self.openai_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"OpenAI client not initialized - missing API key\")\n                \n            if os.getenv(\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"):\n                self.anthropic_client = anthropic.Anthropic(api_key=os.getenv(\"ANTHROPIC_API_KEY\"))\n                logger.info(\"Anthropic client initialized\")\n            else:\n                self.anthropic_client = None\n                logger.warning(\"Anthropic client not initialized - missing API key\")\n                \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to initialize API clients: {e}\")\n            # Set clients to None to avoid further errors\n            self.openai_client = None\n            self.anthropic_client = None\n\n    def get_file_hash(self, file_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate MD5 hash of file contents\"\"\"\n        with open(file_path, \"rb\") as f:\n            return hashlib.md5(f.read()).hexdigest()\n\n    def check_cache(self, file_hash: str) -> Optional[Dict]:\n        \"\"\"Check if file has been processed before\"\"\"\n        cache_file = self.base_dir / \"cache\" / f\"{file_hash}.json\"\n        if cache_file.exists():\n            try:\n                with open(cache_file, \"r\") as f:\n                    cache_data = json.load(f)\n                # Check if cache is still valid (less than 7 days old)\n                cache_date = time.strptime(cache_data[\"timestamp\"], \"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\")\n                cache_time = time.mktime(cache_date)\n                if time.time() - cache_time < 7 * 24 * 3600:  # 7 days\n                    return cache_data\n            except (json.JSONDecodeError, ValueError, KeyError) as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Invalid cache file {cache_file}: {e}\")\n        return None\n\n    def save_to_cache(self, file_hash: str, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save results to cache\"\"\"\n        cache_file = self.base_dir / \"cache\" / f\"{file_hash}.json\"\n        cache_data = {\n            \"timestamp\": time.strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S\"),\n            \"transcript\": transcript,\n            \"analysis\": analysis\n        }\n        try:\n            with open(cache_file, \"w\") as f:\n                json.dump(cache_data, f)\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.warning(f\"Failed to save cache file {cache_file}: {e}\")\n\n    def transcribe_large_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe large audio files by splitting into chunks\"\"\"\n        file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n        file_size_mb = file_size / (1024 * 1024)\n        \n        logger.info(f\"Processing large audio file: {audio_path.name} ({file_size_mb:.1f}MB)\")\n        \n        # Get audio duration\n        try:\n            duration = self.file_handler.get_audio_duration(audio_path)\n            logger.info(f\"Audio duration: {duration:.1f} seconds\")\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Failed to get audio duration: {e}\")\n            return self._transcribe_fallback(audio_path)\n        \n        # Determine chunk size (10 minutes or less to stay under 25MB)\n        chunk_duration = 600  # 10 minutes per chunk (safe for Whisper)\n        \n        # Adjust chunk duration based on file size if needed\n        if file_size_mb > 500:  # Very large files, use smaller chunks\n            chunk_duration = 300  # 5 minutes\n        \n        transcripts = []\n        temp_dir = self.base_dir / \"temp\"\n        temp_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n        \n        # Process in chunks\n        for start_time in range(0, int(duration), chunk_duration):\n            end_time = min(start_time + chunk_duration, duration)\n            \n            # Extract chunk\n            chunk_path = temp_dir / f\"chunk_{start_time}_{audio_path.name}\"\n            try:\n                self.file_handler.extract_audio_chunk(audio_path, chunk_path, start_time, end_time)\n                \n                # Transcribe chunk\n                chunk_transcript = self._transcribe_audio_chunk(chunk_path)\n                transcripts.append(chunk_transcript)\n                \n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f\"Failed to process chunk {start_time}-{end_time}: {e}\")\n                transcripts.append(f\"[Chunk {start_time}-{end_time}s: Transcription failed: {e}]\")\n            \n            # Clean up chunk\n            try:\n                chunk_path.unlink()\n            except:\n                pass\n        \n        return \"\\n\".join(transcripts)\n\n    def _transcribe_audio_chunk(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe a single audio chunk using OpenAI Whisper\"\"\"\n        if not self.openai_client:\n            file_size_mb = audio_path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)\n            return f\"[Chunk: {file_size_mb:.1f}MB - API unavailable]\"\n            \n        try:\n            with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n                transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                    model=\"whisper-1\", \n                    file=audio_file,\n                    response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n                )\n                return \"\\n\".join(\n                    f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start + (float(audio_path.stem.split('_')[1]) if '_' in audio_path.stem else 0))} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end + (float(audio_path.stem.split('_')[1]) if '_' in audio_path.stem else 0))}: {seg.text}\"\n                    for seg in transcript.segments\n                )\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"OpenAI transcription failed for chunk: {e}\")\n            file_size_mb = audio_path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)\n            return f\"[Chunk: {file_size_mb:.1f}MB - Transcription error]\"\n\n    @tenacity.retry(\n        stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n        wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n    )\n    def transcribe_audio(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Transcribe audio using OpenAI Whisper with large file support\"\"\"\n        file_size = audio_path.stat().st_size\n        \n        # For small files (<25MB), use OpenAI directly\n        if file_size <= 24 * 1024 * 1024:  # 24MB to be safe\n            if not self.openai_client:\n                return self._transcribe_fallback(audio_path)\n                \n            try:\n                with open(audio_path, \"rb\") as audio_file:\n                    transcript = self.openai_client.audio.transcriptions.create(\n                        model=\"whisper-1\", \n                        file=audio_file,\n                        response_format=\"verbose_json\"\n                    )\n                    return \"\\n\".join(\n                        f\"{self.format_timestamp(seg.start)} -- {self.format_timestamp(seg.end)}: {seg.text}\"\n                        for seg in transcript.segments\n                    )\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.error(f\"OpenAI transcription failed: {e}\")\n                # Fall through to chunking method\n        \n        # For large files, use chunking\n        return self.transcribe_large_audio(audio_path)\n\n    def _transcribe_fallback(self, audio_path: Path) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Fallback transcription when APIs are unavailable\"\"\"\n        logger.warning(\"Using fallback transcription - API unavailable\")\n        # Return a simple timestamped format\n        file_size_mb = audio_path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)\n        return f\"00:00 -- 01:00: Audio file ({file_size_mb:.1f} MB). Transcription requires OpenAI API key.\"\n\n    @tenacity.retry(\n        stop=tenacity.stop_after_attempt(3),\n        wait=tenacity.wait_exponential(multiplier=1, min=4, max=10)\n    )\n    def analyze_content(self, content: str, context: str = \"\") -> str:\n        \"\"\"Analyze content using best available LLM (Claude preferred, then GPT-4o)\"\"\"\n        # Try Claude first\n        if self.anthropic_client:\n            try:\n                result = self._analyze_claude(content, context)\n                if result and self.validate_analysis_format(result):\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"Claude analysis failed: {e}\")\n        \n        # Fall back to GPT-4o if Claude fails or is unavailable\n        if self.openai_client:\n            try:\n                result = self._analyze_gpt4(content, context)\n                if result and self.validate_analysis_format(result):\n                    return result\n            except Exception as e:\n                logger.warning(f\"GPT-4 analysis failed: {e}\")\n        \n        # Fallback to template if all methods fail\n        return self.generate_analysis_template(content)\n\n    def validate_analysis_format(self, analysis: str) -> bool:\n        \"\"\"Validate the analysis output format\"\"\"\n        required_sections = [\n            \"Central Themes and Messages\",\n            \"Emotional Tone\",\n            \"Narrative Arc\",\n            \"Creator's Intent\",\n            \"Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\",\n            \"Storytelling Techniques\", \n            \"Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\",\n            \"Audience Engagement and Impact\",\n            \"Overall Effectiveness\"\n        ]\n        \n        return all(section in analysis for section in required_sections)\n\n    def generate_analysis_template(self, content: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Generate analysis using template format\"\"\"\n        template = \"\"\"\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\nAnalysis of central themes and messages would appear here.\n\n### 2. Emotional Tone\nAnalysis of emotional tone would appear here.\n\n### 3. Narrative Arc\nAnalysis of narrative arc would appear here.\n\n### 4. Creator's Intent\nAnalysis of creator's intent would appear here.\n\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\nAnalysis of metaphors, symbols, and imagery would appear here.\n\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\nAnalysis of storytelling techniques would appear here.\n\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\nAnalysis of visuals and audio interplay would appear here.\n\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\nAnalysis of audience engagement and impact would appear here.\n\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\nOverall effectiveness assessment would appear here.\n\"\"\"\n        return template\n\n    def _analyze_claude(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using Claude 3.5\"\"\"\n        prompt = f\"\"\"\n        As an expert media analyst, provide comprehensive analysis in this exact format:\n\n        ### 1. Central Themes and Messages\n        [Analyze the central themes and messages]\n\n        ### 2. Emotional Tone\n        [Analyze the emotional tone]\n\n        ### 3. Narrative Arc\n        [Analyze the narrative arc]\n\n        ### 4. Creator's Intent\n        [Analyze the creator's intent]\n\n        ### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\n        [Analyze metaphors, symbols, and imagery]\n\n        ### 6. Storytelling Techniques\n        [Analyze storytelling techniques]\n\n        ### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\n        [Analyze the interplay between visuals and audio]\n\n        ### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\n        [Analyze audience engagement and impact]\n\n        ### 9. Overall Effectiveness\n        [Provide overall assessment of effectiveness]\n\n        Context: {context}\n        Content: {content}\n        \"\"\"\n        \n        try:\n            message = self.anthropic_client.messages.create(\n                model=\"claude-3-5-sonnet-20240620\",\n                max_tokens=2000,\n                messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}]\n            )\n            return message.content[0].text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"Claude analysis failed: {e}\")\n            return None\n\n    def _analyze_gpt4(self, content: str, context: str) -> Optional[str]:\n        \"\"\"Analyze using GPT-4\"\"\"\n        response = self.openai_client.chat.completions.create(\n            model=\"gpt-4o\",\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are an expert media analyst. Provide analysis in the exact format specified with numbered sections.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": f\"Context: {context}\\n\\nAnalyze this content using this exact format:\\n\\n### 1. Central Themes and Messages\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 2. Emotional Tone\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 3. Narrative Arc\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 4. Creator's Intent\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 5. Significant Metaphors, Symbols, and Imagery\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 6. Storytelling Techniques\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 7. Interplay Between Visuals and Audio\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 8. Audience Engagement and Impact\\n[Analysis]\\n\\n### 9. Overall Effectiveness\\n[Analysis]\\n\\nContent: {content}\"}\n            ],\n            max_tokens=1800,\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message.content\n\n    def process_media_file(self, media_path: Path):\n        \"\"\"Process a single media file with large file support\"\"\"\n        logger.info(f\"Processing: {media_path.name}\")\n        \n        try:\n            # Check cache first\n            file_hash = self.get_file_hash(media_path)\n            cached_data = self.check_cache(file_hash)\n            \n            if cached_data:\n                logger.info(f\"Using cached results for {media_path.name}\")\n                self.save_results_formatted(media_path, cached_data[\"transcript\"], cached_data[\"analysis\"])\n                return\n            \n            # For video files, extract audio first\n            transcript = \"\"\n            if media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp4', '.mov', '.avi']:\n                logger.info(f\"Extracting audio from video: {media_path.name}\")\n                audio_path = self.file_handler.extract_audio_from_video(media_path)\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(audio_path)  # This now handles large files\n                # Clean up audio file\n                audio_path.unlink()\n            elif media_path.suffix.lower() in ['.mp3', '.wav', '.m4a']:\n                # For audio files, process directly (with large file support)\n                transcript = self.transcribe_audio(media_path)\n            else:\n                logger.warning(f\"Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\")\n                transcript = f\"00:00 -- 01:00: Unsupported file format: {media_path.suffix}\"\n            \n            # Analyze content\n            analysis = self.analyze_content(transcript, f\"Analysis of {media_path.name}\")\n            \n            # Save results\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            # Save to cache\n            self.save_to_cache(file_hash, transcript, analysis)\n            \n            logger.info(f\"✅ Completed: {media_path.name}\")\n            \n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f\"❌ Failed to process {media_path.name}: {e}\")\n            # Save error result\n            error_transcript = \"00:00 -- 01:00: Error processing file. Please check logs for details.\"\n            error_analysis = self.generate_analysis_template(\"\")\n            self.save_results_formatted(media_path, error_transcript, error_analysis)\n\n    def save_results_formatted(self, media_path: Path, transcript: str, analysis: str):\n        \"\"\"Save analysis results in the specific format requested\"\"\"\n        base_name = media_path.stem\n        \n        # Save in the exact format: Analysis {content} || Transcript {content}\n        formatted_content = f\"Analysis {{{analysis}}} || Transcript {{{transcript}}}\"\n        \n        # Save to analysis directory\n        analysis_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_formatted.txt\"\n        analysis_file.write_text(formatted_content, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        # Also save separate files for transcript and analysis\n        transcript_file = self.base_dir / \"transcripts\" / f\"{base_name}_transcript.txt\"\n        transcript_file.write_text(transcript, encoding='utf-8')\n        \n        analysis_only_file = self.base_dir / \"analysis\" / f\"{base_name}_analysis.txt\"\n        analysis_only_file.write_text(analysis, encoding='utf-8')\n\n    @staticmethod\n    def format_timestamp(seconds: float) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format seconds into MM:SS\"\"\"\n        minutes = int(seconds // 60)\n        seconds = int(seconds % 60)\n        return f\"{minutes:02d}:{seconds:02d}\"\n\n    def process_all_media_files(self):\n        \"\"\"Process all media files with progress tracking\"\"\"\n        media_files = []\n        \n        for ext in ['*.mp3', '*.mp4', '*.wav', '*.m4a', '*.mov', '*.avi']:\n            media_files.extend(self.base_dir.glob(ext))\n        \n        print(f\"Found {len(media_files)} media files\")\n        \n        # Process files with progress bar\n        with tqdm(total=len(media_files), desc=\"Processing files\") as pbar:\n            for media_file in media_files:\n                self.process_media_file(media_file)\n                pbar.update(1)\n                pbar.set_postfix(file=media_file.name[:20])\n\ndef main():\n    \"\"\"Main execution function\"\"\"\n    print(\"=== ULTIMATE Media Analysis Pipeline ===\")\n    print(\"Simplified Edition (GPT-4o and Claude only)\")\n    print(\"With FFmpeg chunking for large files\")\n    \n    base_dir_input = input(\"Enter media directory (press Enter for current): \").strip()\n    base_dir = base_dir_input if base_dir_input else None\n    \n    analyzer = UltimateMediaAnalyzer(base_dir)\n    \n    try:\n        # Process all media files\n        analyzer.process_all_media_files()\n        \n        print(f\"\\n✅ Analysis complete!\")\n        print(\"Check 'transcripts' and 'analysis' folders for results.\")\n        \n    except Exception as e:\n        logger.error(f\"Pipeline failed: {e}\")\n        print(f\"\\n❌ Error: {e}\")\n    finally:\n        # Clean up any remaining temp files\n        analyzer.file_handler.cleanup_temp_files()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    # Check if required packages are installed\n    try:\n        import openai\n        import anthropic\n        from tqdm import tqdm\n        import tenacity\n    except ImportError as e:\n        print(f\"Missing required package: {e}\")\n        print(\"Please install with: pip install openai anthropic python-dotenv tqdm tenacity\")\n        exit(1)\n    \n    # Check if ffmpeg is available\n    try:\n        subprocess.run(['ffmpeg', '-version'], capture_output=True, check=True)\n        subprocess.run(['ffprobe', '-version'], capture_output=True, check=True)\n    except (subprocess.CalledProcessError, FileNotFoundError):\n        print(\"Error: ffmpeg and ffprobe are required but not installed or not in PATH.\")\n        print(\"Install ffmpeg:\")\n        print(\"  Windows: Download from https://ffmpeg.org/\")\n        print(\"  macOS: brew install ffmpeg\")\n        print(\"  Linux: sudo apt install ffmpeg\")\n        exit(1)\n    \n    main()\n```\n\n## Key Features for Large File Handling:\n\n1. **Automatic Chunking**: Files >24MB are automatically split into 10-minute chunks\n2. **FFmpeg Integration**: Uses FFmpeg for audio extraction and chunking\n3. **Duration Detection**: Automatically detects audio duration using ffprobe\n4. **Proper Timestamping**: Maintains correct timestamps across chunks\n5. **Error Handling**: Robust error handling for each chunk\n6. **Memory Efficient**: Processes one chunk at a time\n7. **Cleanup**: Automatically cleans up temporary files\n\n## How It Works:\n\n1. **For videos**: Extracts audio using FFmpeg first\n2. **For large audio**: Splits into 10-minute chunks using FFmpeg\n3. **Each chunk**: Sent to OpenAI Whisper individually\n4. **Results combined**: With proper timestamp adjustments\n5. **Analysis**: Uses Claude or GPT-4 for the final analysis\n\n## Requirements:\n\n```bash\npip install openai anthropic python-dotenv tqdm tenacity\n```\n\nPlus FFmpeg and ffprobe installed on your system.\n\nThis implementation will properly handle your 1GB+ files by chunking them into manageable pieces for the OpenAI API."
          }
        ]
      }
    }
  }
}
```
